# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# INITIAL NATION SET ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: initial-nation-and-city-set
component: initial-nation-set

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for the initial nation set of Civilization.

This layer imports Foundation truth
into explicit seed-world nation planning.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE RULE
# ============================================================

Initial nations are not only builder possibilities.

They are explicit seed-world canonical entities
with fixed initial identity, placement,
major cities, population posture,
industry posture, and governance posture.


# ============================================================
# 3. INCLUDED MAJOR NATIONS
# ============================================================

The initial major nation set includes:

- helios_democratic_kingdom
- nova_commercial_federation
- seiwa_state
- gladia_military_alliance
- orpheus_oceanic_union
- aurelia_federal_republic
- free_cities_union


# ============================================================
# 4. SPECIAL CASES
# ============================================================

aurelia_federal_republic:
- historical / dismantled state in current runtime posture

free_cities_union:
- 12-city union
- no permanent supreme ruler
- governed by inter-city representative council


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Initial nation set is a canonical seed-world layer
based on Foundation truth and world-seed design.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/272.initial-nation-and-city-set/2720002_INITIAL_CITY_SET_ARCHITECTURE.md

status: canonical

scope: initial-nation-and-city-set

prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================

# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for the initial city set of major nations.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE RULE
# ============================================================

Initial cities must be explicit seed-world units.

Major nation city sets must include:
- core cities already fixed by Foundation truth
- expanded support cities for population, housing,
  industry, ports, culture, and infrastructure


# ============================================================
# 3. SPECIAL EXPANSION RULES
# ============================================================

Aurelia city naming:
- eastern / russian-like naming posture
- strong religious-historical tone

Free Cities Union:
- 12-city structure
- no permanent supreme ruler
- each city has its own leader
- federation decisions are made by council deliberation


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Initial city set must support population scale,
housing realism, industry distribution,
and political identity.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/277.anchor-company-naming/2770001_INITIAL_ANCHOR_COMPANY_NAMING_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# INITIAL ANCHOR COMPANY NAMING ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: initial-anchor-company-naming
component: initial-anchor-company-naming

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical naming architecture
for initial anchor companies in Civilization seed-world design.

This layer fixes naming culture by nation
before detailed company-by-city assignment.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE RULE
# ============================================================

Anchor company naming must reflect:
- nation history
- political culture
- industrial identity
- city and regional tradition
- symbolic naming posture

Naming is not random flavor text.
It is part of nation identity design.


# ============================================================
# 3. NATION NAMING POSTURES
# ============================================================

helios_democratic_kingdom:
- large companies often use "Helios"
- kingdom-era symbolic legacy remains visible

nova_commercial_federation:
- merchant-origin, commercial, financial, international naming
- ASIC remains as-is

seiwa_state:
- nation name, city name, ordinary surnames
- practical and credible naming posture
- Ninomiya naming is reserved for the railway company only

gladia_military_alliance:
- American-style English naming
- defense, mobility, force, and contract-security tone

orpheus_oceanic_union:
- founder names must be avoided
- island, port, sea, tide, ritual, brewing, fishery naming posture

free_cities_union:
- surname-based merchant, workshop, port, guild naming posture

aurelia_federal_republic:
- names praising the nation or founder
- state, doctrinal, or old-regime naming tone


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Initial anchor company naming is a nation-specific
seed-world identity layer.


# ============================================================

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/280.infrastructure-seed/2800001_INITIAL_INFRASTRUCTURE_PLACEMENT_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# INITIAL INFRASTRUCTURE PLACEMENT ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: infrastructure-seed
component: initial-infrastructure-placement

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for initial infrastructure placement
in Civilization seed-world planning.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE RULE
# ============================================================

Initial infrastructure placement must reflect:
- nation identity
- city role
- population scale
- zoning posture
- geography and disaster profile
- industry and logistics needs

Infrastructure is not generic utility only.
It is part of national identity and world function.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED DIMENSIONS
# ============================================================

Each nation and city infrastructure seed should define:
- transport infrastructure
- utility infrastructure
- logistics and storage infrastructure
- emergency and resilience infrastructure


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Infrastructure seed is a first-class layer
that binds economy, housing, and governance together.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/296.employment-and-qualification-seed/2960001_INITIAL_EMPLOYMENT_AND_QUALIFICATION_SEED_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# INITIAL EMPLOYMENT AND QUALIFICATION SEED ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: employment-and-qualification-seed
component: initial-employment-and-qualification-seed

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for employment offices,
job-matching facilities,
career support facilities,
qualification testing facilities,
and vocational transition facilities
in Civilization seed-world planning.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE RULE
# ============================================================

Employment and qualification facilities must reflect:
- nation identity
- labor structure
- education posture
- industry posture
- household structure
- youth transition structure
- public and private hiring culture

For Helios specifically:
- historical AI aptitude-based occupational assignment must remain visible
- Helios-linked firms often continue to hire lower and middle strata
  based on aptitude judgment outcomes
- noble-family business succession remains structurally separate
  from aptitude-based hiring logic

For Gladia specifically:
- compulsory service must remain visible as a major labor-market institution
- eligible citizens enter a three-year service period between ages 25 and 28
- rear-support military deployment may occur during compulsory service
- front-line deployment is prohibited during compulsory service
- employer seat preservation, family support, income guarantee,
  substitute employment support, compensation, and return-to-work retraining
  are part of the labor-system design


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED DIMENSIONS
# ============================================================

Each nation and city seed should define:
- employment naming posture
- qualification naming posture
- vocational transition naming posture
- internship and interview support posture
- city-level assignment


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Employment seed must make visible
how students become workers,
how workers change roles,
and how qualifications shape social mobility.

These facilities are not generic welfare objects.
They reveal how each society understands aging,
dependency, dignity, and final support.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED DIMENSIONS
# ============================================================

Each nation and city seed should define:
- eldercare naming posture
- family-care vs facility-care posture
- end-of-life support posture
- retirement support posture
- city-level assignment
- national exceptions if applicable


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Eldercare and end-of-life seed must make visible
how old age is lived,
how dependency is supported,
and how final life stages are institutionally handled.

# ============================================================

- nation identity
- climate and geography
- labor structure
- class structure
- school and company culture
- military influence
- religion and ritual posture
- urban versus island life

These are not decorative fashion notes only.
They reveal hierarchy, duty, belonging, and everyday habit.


# ============================================================

# ============================================================

- everyday clothing posture
- workwear posture
- school uniform posture
- company attire posture
- formalwear posture
- ritualwear posture
- class and district appearance gap posture


# ============================================================

Appearance culture seed must make visible
how hierarchy, profession, ritual, and ordinary life
appear on the body.

# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# EVENT ENGINE ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: event-and-ui-foundation
component: event-engine

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for event triggering,
event branching,
event resolution,
event presentation,
and event persistence
across Civilization seed-world systems.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Every event must separate:

- trigger condition
- availability condition
- player-visible decision
- hidden resolution logic
- result package
- persistence and history

No event may directly mix all layers
into a single opaque block.


# ============================================================
# 3. EVENT PIPELINE
# ============================================================

canonical_event_pipeline:
- trigger_detected
- trigger_validated
- availability_checked
- ui_permission_checked
- template_selected
- player_or_system_decision_resolved
- success_failure_roll_resolved
- result_package_generated
- world_state_applied
- history_record_written


# ============================================================
# 4. EVENT CLASSES
# ============================================================

event_classes:
- life_event
- work_event
- political_event
- crisis_event
- ceremony_event
- social_event
- hidden_background_event
- regime_change_event


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

The event engine must make visible
what the player can choose,
what the system resolves,
and what the world remembers.


# ============================================================

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/330.nation-builder-power-structure-extension/3300001_NATION_BUILDER_POWER_STRUCTURE_EXTENSION_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# NATION BUILDER POWER STRUCTURE EXTENSION ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: nation-builder-power-structure-extension
component: nation-builder-power-structure-extension

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical extension architecture
for Power Structure Builder
inside Nation Builder.

This extension separates:

- constitutional structure definition
- mutable power-scope operation
- regime-change event control

so that election-based states do not allow
ordinary post-creation rewriting
of their constitutional foundation.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Nation Builder must distinguish between:

1. structure definition
2. scope operation
3. regime-change transition

These three layers must never be merged.


# ============================================================
# 3. THREE-LAYER MODEL
# ============================================================

The Power Structure Builder must consist of:

- Structure Locked Layer
- Scope Editable Layer
- Regime Change Event Layer

Their meanings are:

Structure Locked Layer
- constitutional and foundational state design
- defined at nation creation
- locked during normal operation

Scope Editable Layer
- legal operational range of power
- delegation
- emergency activation state
- ministry and authority distribution
- editable after nation creation within allowed rules

Regime Change Event Layer
- exceptional transition layer
- used only by special events
- constitutional reform
- revolution
- coup
- emergency reconstruction
- restoration
- regime collapse


# ============================================================
# 4. LOCK RULE
# ============================================================

For election-based nations,
post-creation editing must not directly modify:

- regime type
- election basis
- legislature existence
- executive selection basis
- judiciary base structure
- constitutional term structure
- amendment base rule

These are structure-layer elements.

Normal post-creation editing may only modify:

- authority scope
- delegation range
- active emergency power state
- ministry-level operational range
- local discretion range
- institutional influence weights
- practical control intensity

if such modification remains legal
within the state's structure definition.


# ============================================================
# 5. UI MODE RULE
# ============================================================

The builder must expose three modes:

A. Constitution Mode
- available at nation creation
- available only through exceptional reform events later
- edits locked structure

B. Governance Operation Mode
- normal post-creation mode
- edits scope only
- cannot alter constitutional foundations

C. Regime Change Mode
- event-only mode
- triggered by explicit reform or collapse conditions
- may unlock structure transition workflows


# ============================================================
# 6. REQUIRED SUBSYSTEMS
# ============================================================

The extension must include:

- State Structure Builder
- Legislature Builder
- Executive Builder
- Judiciary Builder
- Local Governance Builder
- Elite and Influence Builder
- Emergency Rule Builder
- Appointment and Succession Builder
- Validation and Lock Engine


# ============================================================
# 7. COUNTRY FIT
# ============================================================

This model must support at least the following cases:

Helios
- formal monarchy + legislature
- king influence is partly informal
- old noble dominance remains visible

Nova
- formal commercial-federal structure
- finance and ASIC influence must be representable
- structure mostly locked after creation

Seiwa
- bureaucratic legal-administrative state
- procedural structure strongly locked

Gladia
- command-heavy state
- emergency power range is large
- military command influence remains highly editable in scope layer

Orpheus
- weak central union
- island autonomy weights are scope-editable
- core union structure remains locked

Aurelia
- reconstruction or collapse mode may temporarily widen regime-change access

Free Cities Union
- federation-level structure locked
- city autonomy scope strongly editable


# ============================================================
# 8. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

The Power Structure Builder must treat
state form, power operation, and regime transition
as separate canonical layers.


# ============================================================
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/331.legislature-builder/3310001_LEGISLATURE_BUILDER_ARCHITECTURE.md

# ============================================================
# LEGISLATURE BUILDER ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical

component: legislature-builder

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for Legislature Builder
inside Nation Builder and Power Structure Builder.

This builder defines:

- chamber structure
- seat structure
- member selection basis
- legislative authority range
- budget authority
- impeachment authority
- committee structure
- dissolution and term rules


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Legislature Builder must separate:

- constitutional chamber design
- seat allocation logic
- member entry logic
- legislative power scope
- practical political influence

A chamber may exist formally
while real influence is weak.
A chamber may also be structurally weak
but practically dominant.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED SUBSYSTEMS
# ============================================================

The builder must include:

- Chamber Structure Builder
- Seat Composition Builder
- Member Entry Builder
- Legislative Power Builder
- Committee Builder
- Dissolution and Term Builder
- Legislature Influence Builder
- Legislature Validation Engine


# ============================================================
# 4. LAYER OWNERSHIP
# ============================================================

Structure-layer examples:
- unicameral or bicameral
- upper house existence
- lower house existence
- chamber naming
- seat classes
- core legislative powers
- dissolution rule base
- term base

Scope-layer examples:
- current legislature influence strength
- practical veto friction
- committee activity level
- elite capture level
- party discipline strength
- budget negotiation intensity

Transition-layer examples:
- upper house abolition
- emergency suspension
- chamber redesign
- revolutionary reconstitution


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

The Legislature Builder must support
formal democracy,
elite-dominated chamber systems,
federal councils,
city unions,
command-shadow legislatures,
and ceremonial legislatures
without confusing form and reality.


# ============================================================

# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# EXECUTIVE BUILDER ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: executive-builder
component: executive-builder

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for Executive Builder
inside Nation Builder and Power Structure Builder.

This builder defines:

- head of state structure
- head of government structure
- ministry structure
- appointment authority
- decree authority
- emergency authority
- command hierarchy
- practical executive control distribution


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Executive Builder must separate:

- formal executive structure
- legal executive powers
- practical command distribution
- emergency escalation
- informal real-control channels

A state may have a symbolic ruler
with strong informal pressure.
A state may also have a formal cabinet
that is operationally weaker
than command, religion, finance, or bureaucracy.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED SUBSYSTEMS
# ============================================================

The builder must include:

- Head of State Builder
- Head of Government Builder
- Executive Office Builder
- Ministry Structure Builder
- Appointment Authority Builder
- Decree and Order Builder
- Emergency Power Builder
- Command Chain Builder
- Executive Validation Engine


# ============================================================
# 4. LAYER OWNERSHIP
# ============================================================

Structure-layer examples:
- head_of_state_type
- head_of_government_type
- cabinet_exists
- ministry_base_structure
- executive_selection_base
- executive_removal_base
- decree_base_rule
- emergency_power_ceiling
- succession_base_rule

Scope-layer examples:
- current_executive_power_level
- current_ministry_scope_map
- practical_order_intensity
- current_appointment_discretion
- military_command_influence
- bureaucracy_control_intensity
- ruler_informal_pressure_level
- emergency_power_active_state

Transition-layer examples:
- coup_control_mode
- provisional_government_mode
- restoration_mode
- executive_reconstitution_mode
- collapse_administration_mode


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

The Executive Builder must support
symbolic monarchies,
cabinet states,
commercial executives,
command states,
religious rule,
weak federative administrations,
and unstable reconstruction executives
without confusing office form
with real control.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/333.official-executive-and-elite-appointment-builder/3330001_OFFICIAL_EXECUTIVE_AND_ELITE_APPOINTMENT_BUILDER_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# OFFICIAL EXECUTIVE AND ELITE APPOINTMENT BUILDER ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: official-executive-and-elite-appointment-builder
component: official-executive-and-elite-appointment-builder

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for appointment, promotion, confirmation,
retention, removal, and succession
of senior officials, executives, commanders,
religious elites, and quasi-public leadership
in Civilization seed-world planning.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Appointment systems must distinguish between:

- formal appointment authority
- eligibility and qualification rules
- practical influence over selection
- promotion pipeline
- removal and purge logic
- succession continuity

A role may be formally merit-based
but practically patronage-based.
A role may be formally appointed
but effectively reserved for a class,
faction, military lineage, business elite,
or doctrinal circle.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED SUBSYSTEMS
# ============================================================

The builder must include:

- Office Category Builder
- Appointment Rule Builder
- Promotion Pipeline Builder
- Confirmation Builder
- Removal and Discipline Builder
- Succession Continuity Builder
- Influence and Capture Builder
- Validation Engine


# ============================================================
# 4. OFFICE COVERAGE
# ============================================================

The builder must support at least:

- senior bureaucracy
- state enterprise executives
- railway and port executives
- military high command
- police and internal security command
- education leadership
- public health leadership
- religious institution leadership
- reconstruction authority leadership
- city and local executive appointments


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Appointment design must always show
who is formally appointed,
who is practically selectable,
who can block entry,
and who can survive removal.


# ============================================================
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/334.faction-interest-group-and-lobby-builder/3340001_FACTION_INTEREST_GROUP_AND_LOBBY_BUILDER_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# FACTION INTEREST GROUP AND LOBBY BUILDER ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: faction-interest-group-and-lobby-builder
component: faction-interest-group-and-lobby-builder

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical architecture
for factions, interest groups, lobbying channels,
patronage influence, corruption pathways,
and informal power aggregation
in Civilization seed-world planning.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Power aggregation must distinguish between:

- formal political organization
- policy interest groups
- patronage and protection networks
- economic influence channels
- military and doctrine pressure channels
- corruption and covert capture channels

A state may appear formally constitutional
while practical influence is factionally captured.
A state may also appear fragmented
while stable bargaining among groups
quietly structures power.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED SUBSYSTEMS
# ============================================================

The builder must include:

- Faction Type Builder
- Interest Group Builder
- Lobby Channel Builder
- Patronage Network Builder
- Corruption and Capture Builder
- Influence Weight Builder
- Conflict and Coalition Builder
- Validation Engine


# ============================================================
# 4. POWER VISIBILITY RULE
# ============================================================

The builder must separate:

- visible power groups
- semi-visible pressure groups
- hidden selection and capture groups

No nation may be modeled
as purely formal power
if informal power is socially decisive.


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Faction design must always show
who wants what,
how they pressure the state,
and how they survive defeat.


# ============================================================

# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: railway-work-ui
component: railway-work-ui

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical UI architecture
for railway operation work,
including timetable control,
rolling stock control,
maintenance planning,
fare management,
delay handling,
station operation,
and service history persistence.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Railway Work UI must separate:

- route and network context
- timetable planning
- rolling stock allocation
- station operation
- maintenance and infrastructure condition
- disruption response
- fare and demand control
- service result and history

No railway UI should reduce railway operation
to a simple transport action list
without time structure,
capacity logic,
or delay consequences.


# ============================================================
# 3. SUPPORTED RAILWAY OPERATION FAMILIES
# ============================================================

supported_railway_operation_families:
- commuter_rail
- intercity_rail
- freight_rail
- military_support_rail
- frontier_support_rail
- ceremonial_or_prestige_line
- emergency_substitution_operation


# ============================================================
# 4. REQUIRED UI LAYERS
# ============================================================

required_ui_layers:
- network_overview_layer
- timetable_layer
- trainset_allocation_layer
- station_operation_layer
- maintenance_layer
- fare_and_demand_layer
- disruption_response_layer
- ai_assist_layer
- result_summary_layer
- service_history_layer


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Railway UI must make operation feel
scheduled, capacity-bound,
failure-sensitive, and nationally meaningful.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/350.integrated-master/3500001_INTEGRATED_MASTER_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# INTEGRATED MASTER ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: integrated-master
component: integrated-master

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical integrated master layer
for Civilization seed-world design.

This layer consolidates:

- nation identity and variation
- event modifier references
- UI slot references
- job and work references
- quick-reference nation summaries
- cross-nation comparison matrix

into a unified read model
for design, balancing, UI, and future implementation.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Integrated masters must not replace
detailed design documents.

Integrated masters must:

- summarize
- map
- normalize
- cross-reference
- expose lookup-ready structure

Detailed design remains the source layer.
Integrated master remains the reference layer.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED SUBSYSTEMS
# ============================================================

The integrated master layer must include:

- Nation Master
- Event Modifier Master
- UI Slot Master
- Job Master
- Country Quick Reference
- Civilization Society Matrix


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Integrated master documents must make it possible
to understand the whole civilization quickly
without erasing nation-specific depth.

# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: implementation-bridge-master
component: implementation-bridge-master

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical bridge layer
between design masters and future implementation.

This layer connects:

- Nation Builder
- Power Structure Builder
- Legislature Builder
- Executive Builder
- Appointment Builder
- Faction Builder
- Event Engine
- Life Event UI
- Work UI
- Integrated Masters

into lookup-ready implementation mappings.


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

The bridge layer must not redefine domain meaning.

It must only:
- identify
- connect
- normalize
- route
- validate
- fallback

Detailed meaning belongs to source design models.
The bridge layer belongs to implementation lookup logic.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUIRED SUBSYSTEMS
# ============================================================

The bridge layer must include:

- Master Identity Map
- Builder Binding Map
- Event UI Binding Map
- Nation Variation Binding Map
- Permission and Lock Binding Map
- Persistence Binding Map
- AI Assist Binding Map
- Validation and Fallback Binding Map


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

The bridge layer must make it possible
to implement the designed civilization
without losing canonical structure.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/01.civilization-os/020.architecture/360.nation-builder-final-integration/3600001_NATION_BUILDER_FINAL_INTEGRATION_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ============================================================

# ============================================================
# NATION BUILDER FINAL INTEGRATION ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
scope: nation-builder-final-integration
component: nation-builder-final-integration

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

Defines the canonical final integration architecture
for Nation Builder
as the primary civilization-state design system.

This architecture integrates:

- nation identity definition
- geography and settlement definition
- economy and society definition
- culture and daily-life definition
- power structure definition
- legislature, executive, appointment, and faction builders
- lock, validation, preview, and persistence
- integrated master and implementation bridge connection


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Nation Builder must act as
the top-level composition surface,
not as a place that redefines
the meaning of lower builders.

Nation Builder must:
- compose
- route
- lock
- validate
- preview
- persist

Lower builders remain the source of detail.
Nation Builder remains the orchestration surface.


# ============================================================
# 3. LAYER MODEL
# ============================================================

Nation Builder must explicitly separate:

- Foundation Layer
- Structure Locked Layer
- Scope Editable Layer
- Regime Change Layer
- Preview and Summary Layer

Foundation Layer:
- nation identity
- geography
- capital
- population base
- economy base
- culture base

Structure Locked Layer:
- constitutional structure
- legislature structure
- executive structure
- appointment structure
- faction category base

Scope Editable Layer:
- power scope
- practical influence
- ministry scope
- local discretion
- operating intensities

Regime Change Layer:
- constitutional reform
- revolution
- collapse
- reconstruction
- restoration

Preview and Summary Layer:
- quick reference
- matrix position
- signature UI tone
- implementation bridge visibility


# ============================================================
# 4. REQUIRED SUBBUILDERS
# ============================================================

required_subbuilders:
- geography_builder
- population_builder
- economy_builder
- culture_builder
- zoning_builder
- military_builder
- power_structure_builder
- legislature_builder
- executive_builder
- appointment_builder
- faction_builder
- validation_and_lock_engine
- preview_and_summary_engine
- persistence_engine


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

Nation Builder must let a user
construct a nation as one coherent object
without collapsing the distinction between
constitution, operation, and transition.
